***aanleggen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanleggen.html>aanleggen</a> (10584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenleggen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leggen.html>leggen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanleggen.html>aanleggen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to set up, lay out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to construct, to build</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to moor (a boat)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to aim (e.g. a rifle, at a target)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanleggen.html>aanleggen</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:vastmaken.html>vastmaken</a></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanmaak.html>aanmaak</a> (66218)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanmaken.html>aanmaken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanmaak.html>aanmaak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>creation, production</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanpassen.html>aanpassen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to adjust, adapt</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fit, try on</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanranden.html>aanranden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to assault, abuse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ation, -ing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The development to specifically “sexual assault” <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> informed by the phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanranding.html>aanranding</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerbaarheid.html>eerbaarheid</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanranding.html>aanranding</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanrandingen.html>aanrandingen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(A) sexual assault, (an instance of) physical sexual abuse. <span class="defdate">[ca. from 19th c.]</span></li>
<li>An assault, a violent attack. <span class="defdate">[ca. from 17th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanrander.html>aanrander</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">aanrandster</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanranding.html>aanranding</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fysieke.html>fysieke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanval.html>aanval</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doel.html>doel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:seksuele.html>seksuele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:handelingen.html>handelingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dwingen.html>dwingen</a></li></ol>

***aanrijden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanrijden.html>aanrijden</a> (16160)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenrijden</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rijden.html>rijden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanrijden.html>aanrijden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to collide with a vehicle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gister.html>gister</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aangereden.html>aangereden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My mother <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> hit by the <a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a> yesterday.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to arrive driving or riding
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fiets.html>fiets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aangereden.html>aangereden</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My mother <b>arrived</b> by bike.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to depart driving
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aangereden.html>aangereden</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My mother just <b>left for</b> home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although in common use in the southern Netherlands and Flanders, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:aanrijden.html>aanrijden</a></i> in the sense of <i>to depart</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not generally understood outside of those regions.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenschouw</i>, but reinterpreted as a deverbal noun from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwen.html>aanschouwen</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijk.html>aanschouwelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijk.html>aanschouwelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">aanschouwelijkst</b>)

<ol><li>graphical, pictorial</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">visible</span>
<ul><li><b>1838</b>, <i>Noodwendig <a href = vnd.unilang:woordenboek.html>woordenboek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> zamenleving (<a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dames.html>dames</a>). <a href = vnd.unilang:voornamelijk.html>Voornamelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bewerkt.html>bewerkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwen.html>vrouwen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanzienlijke.html>aanzienlijke</a> levensstanden <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschaafde.html>beschaafde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kringen.html>kringen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 6, page 195.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunstenaar.html>kunstenaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> alzoo degeen, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overeenstemming.html>overeenstemming</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> idée <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijk.html>aanschouwelijk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">An artist <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> therefore the person, who brings this correspondence of an idea with the form to fruition in a <b>visible</b> work.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">empirical</span>
<ul><li><b>1947</b>, P. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Schilfaarde, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zin.html>zin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschiedenis.html>geschiedenis</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> wijsgerige <a href = vnd.unilang:bespreking.html>bespreking</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:gang.html>gang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensheid.html>mensheid</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a>. 2, page 248.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">Ten <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgemerkt.html>opgemerkt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> [cultuurwetenschap] <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijk.html>aanschouwelijk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:evenals.html>evenals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:natuurwetenschap.html>natuurwetenschap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanschouwelijke.html>aanschouwelijke</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:betrekking.html>betrekking</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Let it be mentioned in the first place, that the [the humanities] are <b>empirical</b>, just like natural science <a href = vnd.unilang:concerns.html>concerns</a> the <b>empirical</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>

***aanslaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanslaan.html>aanslaan</a> (20635)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenslaen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanslaan.html>aanslaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike physically so as to activate or produce an effect</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tax (a taxable person) with a tax assessment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start, to kick in, to switch on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a dog</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start barking <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">as a sign of <a href = vnd.unilang:alarm.html>alarm</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to succeed, to have an effect</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch on, to become popular
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Constant <a href = vnd.unilang:leest.html>leest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertaling.html>vertaling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> manifest <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echter.html>echter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanslaat.html>aanslaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:publiek.html>publiek</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Constant reads <a href = vnd.unilang:aloud.html>aloud</a> a translation of his manifest there, which however does not at all <b>catch on</b> with the audience.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanslag.html>aanslag</a> (3166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenslach</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aenslaen</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slach</i> (modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanslaan.html>aanslaan</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i>). Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strike, hit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanslag.html>aanslag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanslagen.html>aanslagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanslag.html>aanslagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>deposit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">substance layered on a surface</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jakkes.html>Jakkes</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>zit</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aanslag.html>aanslag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plee.html>plee</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:yuck.html>Yuck</a>, there's <b>scale</b> on the <a href = vnd.unilang:loo.html>loo</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>stroke, keystroke</li>
<li>attack, assault</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of taxes</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> assessment</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aansluiting.html>aansluiting</a> (20159)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aansluiten.html>aansluiten</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aansluiting.html>aansluiting</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aansluitingen.html>aansluitingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aansluiting.html>aansluitinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>junction, connection <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">such as a power junction  |  <i>stroomaansluiting</i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>liaison, relation, connection
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vond.html>vond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weinig.html>weinig</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aansluiting.html>aansluiting</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leerlingen.html>leerlingen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She experienced little of a <b>bond</b> with the other pupils.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>connection, the act of connecting
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afsluiting.html>afsluiting</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">public transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> link or linkage with other public transport lines
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aansluiting.html>aansluiting</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stadsbus.html>stadsbus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:metro.html>metro</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kende.html>kende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruimte.html>ruimte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbetering.html>verbetering</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>interlinkage</b> between city <a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a> and underground <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> some for improvement.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">public transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ride on another public transport line, being compatible with the trip on the preceding line
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trein.html>trein</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gestopt.html>gestopt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vanwege.html>vanwege</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:agressieve.html>agressieve</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dronken.html>dronken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:passagier.html>passagier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gangpad.html>gangpad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaste.html>plaste</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:waardoor.html>waardoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:velen.html>velen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aansluiting.html>aansluiting</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:misten.html>misten</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The train <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> halted because of an aggressive drunk passenger who peed in the corridor, which caused many to miss their <b>rides on other lines</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play (a card) as the first card</li></ol>
